An animal companion’s abilities are determined by the [druid’s](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) level and its animal racial traits. **Table: Animal Companion Base Statistics** determines many of the base statistics of the animal companion. They remain creatures of the animal type for purposes of determining which spells can affect them.

pathfinder-complete-character-chronicles-druid

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1st | 2 | +1 | +3 | +3 | +0 | 2 | 1 | +0 | +0 | 1 | [Link](#TOC-Link-Ex-), [share spells](#TOC-Share-Spells-Ex-) |
| 2nd | 3 | +2 | +3 | +3 | +1 | 3 | 2 | +0 | +0 | 1 | — |
| 3rd | 3 | +2 | +3 | +3 | +1 | 3 | 2 | +2 | +1 | 2 | [Evasion](#TOC-Evasion-Ex-) |
| 4th | 4 | +3 | +4 | +4 | +1 | 4 | 2 | +2 | +1 | 2 | [Ability score increase](#TOC-Ability-Score-Increase-Ex-) |
| 5th | 5 | +3 | +4 | +4 | +1 | 5 | 3 | +2 | +1 | 2 | — |
| 6th | 6 | +4 | +5 | +5 | +2 | 6 | 3 | +4 | +2 | 3 | [Devotion](#TOC-Devotion) |
| 7th | 6 | +4 | +5 | +5 | +2 | 6 | 3 | +4 | +2 | 3 | — |
| 8th | 7 | +5 | +5 | +5 | +2 | 7 | 4 | +4 | +2 | 3 | — |

| 20th | 16 | +12 | +10 | +10 | +5 | 16 | 8 | +12 | +6 | 7 | [Ability score increase](#TOC-Ability-Score-Increase-Ex-) |

#### Class Level

The character’s [druid](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) level. The [druid’s](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) class levels stack with levels of any other classes that are entitled to an animal companion for the purpose of determining the companion’s statistics.

#### HD

This is the total number of eight-sided (d8) Hit Dice the animal companion possesses, each of which gains a [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) modifier, as normal.

FYI: Hit Points and Animal Companions

The following information is from the Pathfinder Society Organized Play FAQ section. We thought it might be helpful information for a player or GM in adjudicating common problems or questions. Usage is up to the GM of your game.

How do I determine hit points for my animal companion?

Animal companions receive average [hit points](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Hit-Points) per hit die. For d8, the average is 4.5. Multiply 4.5 times the number of hit dice your animal companion has and round down. Recalculate [hit points](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Hit-Points) for your companion each time it gains additional hit dice. After its [hit points](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Hit-Points) are calculated, add in appropriate bonuses from its [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) modifier, feats, and so on.

[[Source](https://paizo.com/organizedplay/faq#v5748eaic9vh3)]

#### BAB

This is the animal companion’s [base attack bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Attack-Bonus). An animal companion’s [base attack bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Attack-Bonus) is the same as that of a [druid](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) of a level equal to the animal’s HD. [Animal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/cleric/domains/paizo-domains/animal-domain) companions do not gain additional attacks using their [natural weapons](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) for a high [base attack bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Attack-Bonus).

#### Fort/Ref/Will

These are the animal companion’s base saving throw bonuses. An animal companion has good [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) and [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) saves.

#### Skills

This lists the animal’s total skill ranks. Animal companions can assign skill ranks to any skill listed below. If an animal companion increases its [Intelligence](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) to 10 or higher, it gains bonus skill ranks as normal. Animal companions with an [Intelligence](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) of 3 or higher can purchase ranks in any skill. An animal companion cannot have more ranks in a skill than it has [Hit Dice](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Hit-Dice-HD-).

Animal companions can have ranks in any of the following skills:

[Acrobatics](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/acrobatics)\* (Dex), [Climb](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/climb)\* (Str), [Escape Artist](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/escape-artist) (Dex), [Fly](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/fly)\* (Dex), [Intimidate](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/intimidate) (Cha), [Perception](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/perception)\* (Wis), [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth)\* (Dex), [Survival](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/survival) (Wis), and [Swim](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/swim)\* (Str).

All of the skills marked with an (\*) are class skills for animal companions. Animal companions with an [Intelligence](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) of 3 or higher can put ranks into any skill.

#### Feats

This is the total number of feats possessed by an animal companion. Animal companions should select their feats from those listed under [Animal Feats](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid#TOC-Animal-Feats). Animal companions can select other feats, although they are unable to utilize some feats (such as [Martial Weapon Proficiency](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/martial-weapon-proficiency)). Note that animal companions cannot select a feat with a requirement of [base attack bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Attack-Bonus) +1 until they gain their second feat at 3 [Hit Dice](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Hit-Dice-HD-).

Animal companions can select from the following feats:

[Acrobatic](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/acrobatic), [Agile Maneuvers](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/agile-maneuvers-combat), Armor Proficiency ([light](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/armor-proficiency-light), [medium](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/armor-proficiency-medium), and [heavy](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/armor-proficiency-heavy)), [Athletic](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/athletic), [Blind-Fight](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/blind-fight-combat), [Combat Reflexes](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/combat-reflexes-combat), [Diehard](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/diehard), [Dodge](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/dodge-combat), [Endurance](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/endurance), [Great Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/great-fortitude), [Improved Bull Rush](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/improved-bull-rush-combat), [Improved Initiative](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/improved-initiative-combat), [Improved Natural Armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/monster-feats#improved-natural-armor), [Improved Natural Attack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/monster-feats#improved-natural-attack), [Improved Overrun](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/improved-overrun-combat), [Intimidating Prowess](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/intimidating-prowess-combat), [Iron Will](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/iron-will), [Lightning Reflexes](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/lightning-reflexes), [Mobility](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/mobility-combat), [Power Attack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/power-attack-combat), [Run](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/run), [Skill Focus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/skill-focus), [Spring Attack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/spring-attack-combat), [Stealthy](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/stealthy), [Toughness](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/toughness), [Weapon Finesse](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/weapon-finesse-combat), and [Weapon Focus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/combat-feats/weapon-focus-combat).

Animal companions with an [Intelligence](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) of 3 or higher can select any feat they are physically capable of using. GMs might expand this list to include feats from other sources.

#### Natural Armor Bonus

The number noted here is an improvement to the animal companion’s existing [natural armor bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus).

#### Str/Dex Bonus

Add this value to the animal companion’s [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) and [Dexterity](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) scores.

#### Bonus Tricks

The value given in this column is the total number of “bonus” tricks that the animal knows in addition to any that the [druid](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) might choose to teach it (see the [Handle Animal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/handle-animal) skill). These bonus tricks don’t require any training time or [Handle Animal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/handle-animal) checks, and they don’t count against the normal limit of tricks known by the animal. The [druid](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) selects these bonus tricks, and once selected, they can’t be changed.

#### Link (Ex)

A [druid](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) can handle her animal companion as a [free action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Free-Actions), or [push](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Push-Ex-) it as a [move action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Move-Actions), even if she doesn’t have any ranks in the [Handle Animal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/handle-animal) skill. The [druid](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) gains a +4 [circumstance bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Circumstance-Bonus) on all [wild empathy](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid#TOC-Wild-Empathy-Ex-) checks and [Handle Animal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/handle-animal) checks made regarding an animal companion.

#### Share Spells (Ex)

The [druid](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) may cast a spell with a target of “You” on her animal companion (as a [touch](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Touch-Attacks) range spell) instead of on herself. A [druid](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) may cast spells on her animal companion even if the spells normally do not affect creatures of the companion’s type (animal). Spells cast in this way must come from a class that grants an animal companion. This ability does not allow the animal to share abilities that are not spells, even if they function like spells.

#### Evasion (Ex)

If an animal companion is subjected to an attack that normally allows a [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) saving throw for half damage, it takes no damage if it makes a successful saving throw.

#### Devotion

An animal companion gains a +4 [morale bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Morale-Bonus) on [Will](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Will) saves against [enchantment](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic#TOC-Enchantment) spells and effects.

#### Ability Score Increase (Ex)

The animal companion adds +1 to any one of its ability scores.

#### Multiattack

An animal companion gains [Multiattack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/monster-feats#TOC-Multiattack-Combat-) as a bonus feat if it has three or more [natural attacks](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) and does not already have that feat. If it does not have the requisite three or more [natural attacks](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks), the animal companion instead gains a second attack with its primary [natural weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks), albeit at a –5 penalty.

#### Improved Evasion (Ex)

When subjected to an attack that normally allows a [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) saving throw for half damage, an animal companion takes no damage if it makes a successful saving throw and only half damage if the saving throw fails.

### Magic Items

Animal Companions only have specific magic item slots available to them. Their magic item slots are based on their general body form. The table can be found [here](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/Magic-items/#table-magic-item-slots-for-animals).

### Animal Companion Descriptions

Animal companions listed in order of effective druid level can be found [here](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid/animal-companions/npc-codex-appendix-1-animal-companions)

Each animal companion has different starting sizes, speed, attacks, ability scores, and special qualities. All animal attacks are made using the creature’s full [base attack bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Attack-Bonus) unless otherwise noted. Animal attacks add the animal’s [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) modifier to the damage roll, unless it is its only attack, in which case it adds 1-1/2 its [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) modifier. Some have special abilities, such as [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent). As you gain levels, your animal companion improves as well, usually at 4th or 7th level, in addition to the standard bonuses noted on **Table: Animal Companion Base Statistics**. Instead of taking the listed benefit at 4th or 7th level, you can instead choose to increase the companion’s [Dexterity](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) and [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) by 2.

#### Allosaurus

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium, **Speed** 40 ft.; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6), 2 claws (1d4); **Ability Scores** **Str** 14, **Dex** 16, **Con** 10, **Int** 2, **Wis** 15, **Cha** 10; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent).

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8), 2 claws (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** +8, **Dex** –2, **Con** +4; **Special Qualities** [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-), [pounce](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Pounce-Ex-).

#### Amargasaurus

[Source](https://amzn.to/44Y2HXU)

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 30 ft.; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** slam (1d6), tail slap (1d6); **Ability Scores [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-)** 11, **Dex** 18, **Con** 9, **Int** 2, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 10; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent).

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** slam (1d8), tail slap (1d8); **Ability Scores [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-)** +8, **Dex** –2, **Con** +4; **Special Qualities** [trample](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Trample-Ex-).

#### Anglerfish

[[Source](http://amzn.to/2z71S07)]

The anglerfish is a fish that uses a bioluminescent lure at the tip of a stalk protruding from its head to attract prey.

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** swim 40 ft.; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** **Str** 13, **Dex** 15, **Con** 12, **Int** 1, **Wis** 12, **Cha** 2; **Special Qualities** [aquatic](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Aquatic), [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-) (Medium), [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), lure (sheds light as per a [candle](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/equipment/goods-and-services/hunting-camping-survival-gear#TOC-Candle)), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent).

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (2d6 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** **Str** +2, **Dex** –2, **Con** +4; **Special Qualities** [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-) (Large), [swallow whole](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Swallow-Whole-Ex-) (Medium).

#### Ankylosaurus

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 30 ft.; **AC** +9 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** tail (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** 10, **Dex** 14, **Con** 9, **Int** 2, **Wis** 12, **Cha** 8; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent).

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** tail (2d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** +8, **Dex** –2, **Con** +4; **Special Qualities** [stun](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Stunned).

Stun (Ex)

The ankylosaurus’s tail can deliver a powerful, stunning blow. A creature struck by this attack must make a DC (10 + 1/2 HD + Str modifier) [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) save or be [dazed](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Dazed) for 1 round. If the strike is a [critical hit](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Critical-Hits) and the target fails its save, it is instead [stunned](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Stunned) for 1d4 rounds.

#### Aurochs

Starting Statistics

**Size** Large; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** gore (1d8); **Ability Scores** **Str** +8, **Dex** –2, **Con** +4; **Special Qualities** stampede, [trample](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Trample-Ex-).

Stampede (Ex)

A stampede occurs if three or more creatures with stampede make a [trample](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Trample-Ex-) attack while remaining adjacent to each other. While stampeding, the creatures can [trample](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Trample-Ex-) foes of their [size](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Size-Bonus) or smaller, and the [trample’s](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Trample-Ex-) save DC increases by +2.

#### Axe Beak

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 50 ft.; **Attack** bite (1d6 + 1-1/2 **Str**); **Ability Scores** **Str** 10, **Dex** 17, **Con** 12, **Int** 2, **Wis** 11, **Cha** 10; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision).

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8 + 1-1/2 **Str**); **Ability Scores** **Str** +8, **Dex** –2, **Con** +4; **Special Attacks** sudden [charge](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Charge).

Sudden Charge (Ex)

When making a [charge](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Charge) attack, an axe beak makes a single bite attack. If successful, it may also attempt to [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip) its opponent as a [free action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Free-Actions) without provoking an [attack of opportunity](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Attacks-of-Opportunity). If the attempt fails, the axe beak cannot be [tripped](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip) in return.

Those hit by a bristle boar’s gore attack must succeed at a [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) saving throw to avoid being speared by the dangerously sharp spines around its head and neck. Failure results in 1d4 points of piercing damage.

Starting Statistics

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite 2d6; **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +4; **Special Qualities** blood rage\*, [ferocity](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Ferocity-Ex-).

**\*Blood Rage** When a ceratosaurus takes damage in combat, on its next turn it can fly into a rage as a free action. It gains +2 [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) and +2 [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-), but takes a –2 penalty to its AC. The rage lasts as long as the battle or 1 minute, whichever is shorter. It cannot end its rage voluntarily.

#### Chameleon, Giant

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 30 ft., climb 30 ft.; **Attack** bite (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** 12, **Dex** 14, **Con** 14, **Int** 2, **Wis** 11, **Cha** 7; **Special Qualities** +10 [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth) when still, [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision).

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **Speed** 40 ft., climb 40 ft.; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** –2, **Con** +2; **Special Attacks** [pull](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Pull-Ex-) (tongue, 5 ft.), tongue.

Tongue (Ex)

A giant chameleon can [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-) a foe with its tongue and draw the victim to its mouth. This tongue attack has a reach of 15 feet. The attack does no damage, but allows the creature to [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-). A giant chameleon does not gain the [grappled](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Grappled) condition while using its tongue in this manner.

#### Crocodile

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 20 ft., swim 30 ft.; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** **Str** 15, **Dex** 14, **Con** 15, **Int** 1, **Wis** 12, **Cha** 2; **Special Qualities** [hold breath](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Hold-Breath-Ex-), [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision).

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; **Attack** bite (1d8) or tail slap (1d12); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** –2, **Con** +2; **Special Attacks** death roll, sprint.

Death Roll (Ex)

When [grappling](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple) a foe of its size or smaller, a crocodile can perform a death roll upon making a successful [grapple](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple) check. As it clings to its foe, it tucks in its legs and rolls rapidly, twisting and wrenching its victim. The crocodile inflicts its bite damage and knocks the creature [prone](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Prone). If successful, the crocodile maintains its [grapple](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple).

Hold Breath (Ex)

A crocodile can hold its breath for a number of rounds equal to 4 times its [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) score before it risks drowning.

Sprint (Ex)

Once per minute a crocodile may sprint, increasing its land speed to 40 feet for 1 round.

#### Deinotherium

[[Source](https://amzn.to/44Y2HXU)]

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 30 ft.; **AC** +4 [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** slam (1d6), gore (1d8); **Ability Scores** **Str** 14, **Dex** 10, **Con** 15, **Int** 2, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 3; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent).

Sweep (Ex)

A deinotherium can sweep a target with its downward-curving tusks and knock the victim to the ground. As part of a charge, a deinotherium can move up to twice its base speed in a straight line and make a gore attack at any point during its movement. If this attack is successful, the target is knocked [prone](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Prone) and the deinotherium can deal damage with its [trample](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Trample-Ex-) attack before continuing its movement.

**Source**: [PRG:B4](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1601255756/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_il_tl?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1601255756&linkCode=as2&tag=httpwwwd20pfs-20)

**Size** Medium; **Attack** bite (1d6 plus [disease](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/diseases)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +4, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2

Filth Fever Disease

Method-injury (bite); *save* fortitude, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC; *onset* 1d3 days; *frequency* 1/day; *effect* 1d3 [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) damage and 1d3 [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) damage; *cure* 2 consecutive saves

Lesser Compression (Ex)

A dire raccoon can move through an area as small as one-half its space without squeezing or onequarter its space when squeezing.

Opportunistic Bite (Ex)

On a successful bite attack against an opponent it’s [flanking](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Flanking) or that is denied its [Dexterity](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) bonus to AC, a jackal deals 1 additional point of damage.

Cute as Heck (Ex)

A dire corgi, despite its size and [ferocity](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Ferocity-Ex-), is really cute. It considers [Diplomacy](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/diplomacy) as a class skill and may make [Diplomacy](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/diplomacy) checks in any social situation as an innate trick. Additionally, any time their master uses the [Diplomacy](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/diplomacy) skill, the dire corgi automatically attempts an [Aid](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/a/aid) Another check, even if they are rolling their own [Diplomacy](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/diplomacy) attempt.

#### Eohippus

[[Source](http://amzn.to/2z71S07)]

The eohippus is a small, primeval ancestor of the modern horse. It has three-toed feet rather than hooves.

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 40 ft.; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d4); **Ability Scores** **Str** 11, **Dex** 15, **Con** 12, **Int** 2, **Wis** 11, **Cha** 4; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent).

4th-Level Advancement

**Ability Scores** **Dex** +2, **Con** +2.

#### Frog, Giant

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 30 ft.,swim 30 ft.; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** 15, **Dex** 13, **Con** 16, **Int** 1, **Wis** 9, **Cha** 6; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent), tongue, [pull](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Pull-Ex-).

Tongue (Ex)

A giant frog’s tongue is a primary attack with reach equal to three times the frog’s normal reach (15 feet for a Medium giant frog). A giant frog’s tongue deals no damage on a hit, but can be used to [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-). A giant frog does not gain the [grappled](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Grappled) condition while using its tongue in this manner.

4th-Level Advancement

**Ability Scores** **Str** +2, **Dex** +2; **Special Qualities** [swallow whole](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Swallow-Whole-Ex-).

#### Gecko, Giant

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 30 ft.; **Attack** bite (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** 11, **Dex** 15, **Con** 12, **Int** 2, **Wis** 14, **Cha** 7; **Special Qualities** expert climber, [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision).

Expert Climber (Ex)

A gecko’s feet allow it to climb virtually any surface, no matter how slick or sheer. In effect, geckos are treated as constantly being under a natural version of the spell [spider climb](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/s/spider-climb).

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 40 ft.; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (2d4); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** –2, **Con** +2.

#### Giant Hamster

**[[Source](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-animal-companions-i)]**

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 20 ft., [burrow](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Burrow-Ex-) 10 ft.; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 11, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 15, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 12, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 1, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 12, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 6; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision); **Special Attacks** cheek pouch; **Immune** [disease](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/diseases)

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +4

Cheek Pouch (Ex)

A [giant hamster](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/animals/hamster-giant) can try to stuff a grabbed opponent of two sizes smaller than itself into its cheek pouch by making a successful [grapple](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple) check. A creature stuffed into the [giant hamster](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/animals/hamster-giant)’s cheek pouch takes no damage, and can escape by making a successful [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) check or can cut its way out by using a light slashing or piercing weapon to deal 10 points of damage to the cheek (AC equal to 10 + ½ the [giant hamster](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/animals/hamster-giant)’s [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus)). Once the creature exits, muscular action closes the hole; another trapped opponent must cut its own way out. A [Medium](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/alternative-rule-systems/occult-adventures/occult-classes/medium)-sized [giant hamster](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/animals/hamster-giant) can hold 1 Tiny, 2 Diminutive or 8 Fine creatures in its pouch. A Largesized [giant hamster](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/animals/hamster-giant) can hold 1 Small, 2 Tiny or 8 Diminutive or smaller creatures in its pouch. The [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) check DC is [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-)-based.

#### Giant Porcupine

**[[Source](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-animal-companions-i)]**

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 40 ft.; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** tail slap (1d8); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 13, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 14, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 14, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 2, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 13, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 5; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision); **Defensive Abilities** quills

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; **Attack** tail slap (2d6); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +4, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2

Quills (Ex)

Any creature attacking a [giant](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Giant) porcupine with light or one-handed melee weapons or with melee [natural weapons](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks), or an [unarmed strike](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/equipment/weapons/weapon-descriptions/strike-unarmed) takes 1d3 piercing damage. A creature that grapples a [giant](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Giant) porcupine takes 2d4 piercing damage each round it does so. This damage does not apply if the porcupine grapples a creature.

#### Goblin Dog

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 50 ft.; **Attack** bite (1d4); **Ability Scores** **Str** 11, **Dex** 16, **Con** 11, **Int** 2, **Wis** 12, **Cha** 8; **Special Qualities** allergic reaction, [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent).

Allergic Reaction (Ex)

A goblin dog’s dander is highly irritating to all creatures save those with the [goblinoid subtype](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Goblinoid). A non-goblinoid creature damaged by a goblin dog’s bite, who deals damage to a goblin dog with a [natural weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) or unarmed attack, or who otherwise comes into contact with a goblin dog (including attempts to [grapple](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple) or ride the creature) must make a DC (10 + 1/2 [Hit Dice](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Hit-Dice-HD-) + [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) modifier) [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) save or break out in an itching rash. A creature affected by this rash takes a –2 penalty to [Dexterity](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) and [Charisma](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) for 1 day (multiple allergic reactions do not stack). [*Remove disease*](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/r/remove-disease) or any magical [healing](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic#TOC-Conjuration-Healing) removes the rash instantly. This is a [disease](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/diseases) effect.

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** –2, **Con** +4.

#### Heron, Yolubilis

**Source** [PAP97](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1601257686/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_il_tl?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1601257686&linkCode=as2&tag=httpwwwd20pfs-20&linkId=4VNPUECIQAKY7WNH)

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 30 ft., fly 60 ft. (average); **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 13, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 15, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 14, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 2, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 12, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 9; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision).

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (2d6); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) –2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2; **Special Attacks** still predator.

Still Predator (Ex)

A Yolubilis heron has the ability to stand perfectly still for hours at a time while awaiting prey, making it easy to mistake the bird’s legs for slim tree trunks. A Yolubilis heron can use the [freeze](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Freeze-Ex-) ability while adjacent to trees or any vegetation that could conceal its upper body. While standing in water, it can use the [freeze](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Freeze-Ex-) ability against submerged creatures. Other creatures with low [Intelligence](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) scores or poor senses might be tricked by this ability as well.

#### Hippopotamus

Starting Statistics

#### Hyaenodon

**[[Source](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-animal-companions-i)]**

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 40 ft.; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6 plus [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip) and bone-breaker); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 17, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 17, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 14, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 2, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 13, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 6; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent), racial skill bonus: +4 [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth) in tall grass, +4 [Survival](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/survival) when tracking by [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent)

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8 plus [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip) and bone-breaker); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +4

Bone-breaker (Ex)

A creature that is bit by a [hyaenodon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/animals/hyena/hyaenodon) must make a [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) *save* or suffer a -1 penalty on [attack rolls](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Attack-Roll), damage rolls and [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-)– or [Dexterity](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-)-based skills and checks until they receive [healing](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic#TOC-Conjuration-Healing) or they recover the damage dealt by the [hyaenodon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/animals/hyena/hyaenodon)’s bite naturally. The *save* DC is [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-)-based.

#### Hypersloth

[[Source](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/call-of-the-wild-book-1-the-druid)]

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 10 ft, climb 40 ft; **AC** +2 natural armor; **Attack** 2 claws (1d4)

**Ability Scores** **Str** 10, **Dex** 17, **Con** 12, **Int** 2, **Wis** 14, **Cha** 6

**Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision).

7th-Level Advancement

**Attack** 4 claws (1d4); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/using-ability-scores#TOC-Strength) +2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/using-ability-scores#TOC-Constitution)+2

Burst of Speed (Su)

A hypersloth can act as though under the effect of a [haste](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/h/haste) spell for a number of rounds per day equal to its [Hit Dice](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Hit-Dice-HD-). These rounds can be broken up over multiple uses or used all at once.

An iguanodon’s thumb spikes can inflict grievous wounds—they deal triple damage on a successful [critical hit](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Critical-Hits).

#### Onwu Azu

**[[Source](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-animal-companions-i)]**

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 5 ft. swim 70 ft.; **Attack** bite (1d4 plus [attach](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Attach-Ex-) and [bleed](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Bleed)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 12, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 16, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 12, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 1, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 13, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 6; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [keen scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Keen-Scent-Ex-), racial skill bonus: +8 [Swim](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/swim), [ferocity](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Ferocity-Ex-), [glide](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/g/glide); [CMD](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Combat-Maneuver-Defense) can’t be [tripped](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip).

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; **Attack** bite (1d6 plus [attach](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Attach-Ex-) and [bleed](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Bleed)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +4, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2

Attach (Ex)

When an onwu azu hits with a bite attack, it automatically grapples its foe, though the target isn’t considered to be [grappling](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple) the onwu azu. Each round the onwu azu is [grappling](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple) its foe, it automatically deals its bite damage.

Glide (Ex)

An onwu azu can launch itself into the air and [glide](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/g/glide) for up to 1 minute (depending on the water and weather conditions [GM’s discretion]). When gliding, it has a fly speed of 60 feet with clumsy maneuverability and gains [Flyby Attack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/monster-feats/flyby-attack).

Keen Scent (Ex)

An onwu azu can notice creatures by [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent) within a 180-foot radius underwater and can detect blood in the water at ranges of up to 1 mile.

#### Ostrich

**Source** [PCS:OLoP](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1601255950/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_il_tl?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1601255950&linkCode=as2&tag=httpwwwd20pfs-20)

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 40 ft.; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** claw (1d4); **Ability Scores** **Str** 13, **Dex** 16, **Con** 12, **Int** 2, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 11; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision).

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 60 ft.; **Attack** claw (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** –2, **Con** +2; **Special Qualities** crouch.

Crouch (Ex)

An ostrich can [hide in plain sight](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/rogue/rogue-talents/paizo-rogue-advanced-talents/hide-in-plain-sight-ex) as a bush or shrub by crouching down and concealing its head and legs. It makes a [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth) check as normal, but anyone who observes it from within 30 feet automatically sees through the ruse.

#### Pachycephalosaurus

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 30 ft.; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** gore (1d8); **Ability Scores** **Str** 15, **Dex** 16, **Con** 13, **Int** 2, **Wis** 12, **Cha** 5.

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** gore (1d10); **Ability Scores** **Str** +8, **Dex** –2, **Con** +4; **Special Attacks** clobbering charge.

Clobbering Charge (Ex)

When a pachycephalosaurus hits a target with its slam attack at the end of a [charge](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Charge), it can initiate a [bull rush](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Bull-Rush) as a [free action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Free-Actions) to move the struck target back in the same direction as the [dinosaur’s](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/animals/dinosaur) [charge](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Charge). The pachycephalosaurus cannot move with the target of the [bull rush](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Bull-Rush). If a pachycephalosaurus scores a [critical hit](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Critical-Hits) against a creature with its slam attack at the end of a [charge](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Charge), it also staggers the target for 1 round. If the victim succeeds at a DC 18 [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) save, the stagger effect is negated, but the victim still suffers the effects of the [dinosaur’s](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/animals/dinosaur) [bull rush](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Bull-Rush) attempt. The save DC is [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-)-based.

Razor Scales (Ex)

A dire pangolin’s scales come to fine slicing edges. A creature that strikes a dire pangolin while it is taking a [total defense](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Total-Defense) action with a melee weapon, an [unarmed strike](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/equipment/weapons/weapon-descriptions/strike-unarmed), or a [natural weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) takes 1d8 + [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) modifier points of slashing damage. Melee weapons with reach do not endanger a user in this way.

#### Prionosuchus

[[Source](http://amzn.to/2z71S07)]

This primeval [crocodile](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/animals/crocodile) is equally effective in the water and on land. Its jaws are capable of crushing things with great force.

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 20 ft., swim 30 ft.; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** **Str** 13, **Dex** 14, **Con** 15, **Int** 1, **Wis** 12, **Cha** 4; **Special Attacks** [constrict](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Constrict-Ex-) (1d8); **Special Qualities** [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent).

#### Roc

Rocs taken as animal companions by [druids](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) or [rangers](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/ranger) are typically newly hatched birds—a baby roc is the size of a person and ready for flight and hunting within minutes of hatching. Unfortunately for [druids](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) seeking animal companions of legendary size, an animal companion roc is limited to Large size—still large enough for a Medium [druid](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) or [ranger](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/ranger) to use the flying beast as a mount.

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **AC** +5 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Speed** 20 ft., fly 80 ft.; **Attack** 2 talons (1d4), bite (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** 12, **Dex** 19, **Con** 9, **Int** 2, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 11; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision).

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** 2 talons (1d6 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)), bite (1d8); **Ability Scores** **Str** +8, **Dex** –2, **Con** +4.

#### Shrike, Impaler

**Source** [PAP97](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1601257686/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_il_tl?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1601257686&linkCode=as2&tag=httpwwwd20pfs-20&linkId=4VNPUECIQAKY7WNH)

Impale (Ex)

When an impaler shrike has a creature at least one size smaller than itself [grappled](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Grappled) in its beak, it can move the creature to a dangerous location, such as a spike or a [broken](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Broken) tree limb. This works like the [reposition](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reposition) [combat maneuver](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Combat-Maneuvers), except the shrike can move an opponent to an occupied square. An impaler shrike still provokes an [attack of opportunity](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Attacks-of-Opportunity) using this ability, so it typically pins its victim before attempting this maneuver. As part of this [reposition](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reposition), an impaler shrike can attempt a melee [touch attack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Touch-Attacks) against an AC of 15 to impale the victim on a nearby spike or similar object. If this attack is successful, the victim takes an amount of piercing damage appropriate for the impaling object’s size.

#### Skittergoat

[[Source](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1601257252/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_il_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=1601257252&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=httpwwwd20pfs-20&amp;linkId=KQLONM2S3X3G3MVE)]

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 30 ft.; **AC** +1 [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** gore (1d4); **Ability Scores** **Str** 13, **Dex** 14, **Con** 11, **Int** 2, **Wis** 10, **Cha** 5; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision).

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; **Attack** gore (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** –2, **Con** +2; **Special Qualities** egg cracker.

Egg Cracker (Ex)

A skittergoat’s horns are able to crack through the tough shells of [ankheg](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listin/magical-beasts/ankheg) eggs. When a skittergoat charges, its gore attack is resolved against the target’s [touch](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Touch-Attacks) AC. In addition, when breaking an object, a skittergoat ignores 1 point of the object’s [hardness](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/equipment/damaging-objects#TOC-Hardness).

Poison Skin (Ex)

A creature that strikes a giant toad with an [unarmed strike](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/equipment/weapons/weapon-descriptions/strike-unarmed) or [natural weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) exposes itself to the toad’s poisonous skin.

**Size** Large; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** gore (1d8); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** –2, **Con** +4; **Special Abilities** spit, [trample](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Trample-Ex-).

#### Yak

[[Source](http://amzn.to/2z71S07)]

Stout and stubborn, the yak is sure footed and dependable in rough terrain.

Starting Statistics
