The hooves are primary attacks.

### Aberration Companions

#### Akata

**Prerequisite(s)**: Elder Voice feat, [Knowledge](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/knowledge) (planes) 5

**Note** This companion is available if the Elder Voice feat is taken. The 11th-level mastery benefit is given if the character takes the Elder Voice Mastery feat. Both can be found in Legendary Companions by Legendary Games.

**Source** [SwA:AC](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-aberration-companions-i)

STARTING STATISTICS

**Size** Small; **Speed** 40 ft., climb 20 ft.; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** bite (1d4), 2 tentacles (1d2); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 17, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 14, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 3, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 12, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 11; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 120 ft., [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent), [no breath](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-No-Breath-Ex-), racial skill bonus: +4 [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth); Immune cold, [disease](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/diseases), [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison); **Resist** fire 30; Weaknesses [deaf](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Deafened), vulnerable to salt water

8th-LEVEL ADVANCEMENT

**Size** Medium; **Attack(s)** bite (1d6 plus void bite), 2 tentacles (1d3); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +4, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2

Deaf (Ex)

Akatas cannot hear. They are immune to spells or effects that rely on hearing but they also cannot make [Perception](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/perception) checks to listen.

Salt Water Vulnerability (Ex)

Salt water acts as an acid to akatas. A splash of salt water deals 1d6 points of damage, and full immersion in salt water deals 4d6 points of damage per round.

Void Bite (Ex)

Akatas have a multitude of [invisible](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Invisible) young within their mouths, spreading to hosts through their bites. Only [humanoids](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Humanoid) make suitable hosts for the [akata](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/aberrations/akata) larvae. All other creatures are immune to this [disease](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/diseases).

Disease (Ex)

Void Death: Bite-injury; *save* [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude), [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC; *onset* 1 hour; *frequency* 1/day; *effect* 1d2 [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) and 1d2 [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) damage. An infected creature that dies rises as a [void zombie](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/undead/zombie/void-zombie) 2d4 hours later; *cure* 2 consecutive saves.

#### Bogwid

**Prerequisite(s)**: Elder Voice feat

**Note** This companion is available if the Elder Voice feat is taken. The 11th-level mastery benefit is given if the character takes the Elder Voice Mastery feat. Both can be found in Legendary Companions by Legendary Games.

**Source** [SwA:AC](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-aberration-companions-i)

**Prerequisite(s)**: [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) +4

STARTING STATISTICS

**Size** Small; **Speed** 30 ft., climb 20 ft., swim 20 ft.; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** 2 slams (1d4); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 15, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 20, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 16, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 3, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 4, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 13; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft.; **Resist** acid 5, cold 5; **CMD** +12 vs. [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip); **Special Attacks** [nauseating](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Nauseated) [touch](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Touch-Attacks)

9th-LEVEL ADVANCEMENT

**Size** Medium; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** 2 slams (1d6); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +4, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2; **Special Attacks** revolting aura

MASTERY (13th-Level)

**Special Attacks** ravenous young, [disease](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/diseases)

Nauseating Touch (Ex)

The bogwid’s [touch](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Touch-Attacks) is disgusting. Creatures hit by its slam attack must succeed at a [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) save or be [nauseated](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Nauseated) for 1 round. The save DC is [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based.

Revolting Aura (Ex)

The bogwid is both visually and odoriferously revolting. Any creature within 10 feet of a bogwid must succeed at a [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) save or be [sickened](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Sickened). This effect persists as long as the creature is within the aura and for 2 rounds thereafter. A creature that successfully saves is not subject to the same bogwid’s revolting aura for 24 hours. The save DC is [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based.

Ravenous Young (Ex)

Each round, a bogwid can launch one of the offspring clinging to its back at a target within 10 feet as a ranged [touch attack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Touch-Attacks). On a successful hit, the offspring attaches itself to the target and begins draining blood, automatically dealing 1d2 points of [bleed](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Bleed) damage each round (and possibly infecting the target with bogwid fever, see below). As a [full-round action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Full-Round-Actions), a creature can attempt to remove one of these offspring, either by bludgeoning it with a fist or pulling it off. Either way, removing an offspring kills the larval creature. Someone other than the target the offspring is attached to can also perform this action. Anyone using a weapon to kill or remove an attached offspring deals half of the damage to the creature to which the offspring is attached. A bogwid can launch up to 10 offspring per day before it must rest and gestate more larval young.

Disease (Ex)

Bogwid Fever: Bite—injury; *save* [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude), [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC, onset 1 day, frequency 1/day, effect 1d2 [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) damage and [shaken](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Shaken), cure 2 consecutive saves.

#### Carrion Moth

**Prerequisite(s)**: Elder Voice feat, [Will](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Will) +4

**Note** This companion is available if the Elder Voice feat is taken. The 11th-level mastery benefit is given if the character takes the Elder Voice Mastery feat. Both can be found in Legendary Companions by Legendary Games.

**Source** [SwA:AC](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-aberration-companions-i)

STARTING STATISTICS

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 30 ft., climb 15 ft., fly 60 ft. (good); **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** bite (2d6); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 20, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 10, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 1, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 16, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 6; **Special Qualities** [stench](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Stench-Ex-); **Special Attacks** drone

7th-LEVEL ADVANCEMENT

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** bite (2d8); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +4

MASTERY (11th-Level)

Attack 4 tentacles secondary [natural attacks](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) ([paralysis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Paralysis)); **Special Attacks** [Paralysis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Paralysis-Ex-or-Su-) (2d6 rounds, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC)

Drone (Ex)

The flapping wings of a [carrion moth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/aberrations/carrion-moth) emit a mind-numbing drone that affects all creatures within 80 feet that hear it. Affected creatures must succeed on a [Will](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Will) save or become [confused](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Confused) for 2d4 rounds. A creature that successfully saves cannot be affected by the same [carrion moth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/aberrations/carrion-moth)’s drone attack for 24 hours. The save DC is [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based.

Stench (Ex)

When a [carrion moth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/aberrations/carrion-moth) dies, its carcass splits open and releases a foul-smelling gas. All living creatures (except other [carrion moths](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/aberrations/carrion-moth)) within 5 feet of the carcass must succeed on a [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) save or be [nauseated](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Nauseated) for 1d4+1 rounds. A [delay poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/d/delay-poison) or [neutralize poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/n/neutralize-poison) spell removes the effect from the [nauseated](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Nauseated) creature. This is a [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison) effect. The save DC is [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based.

#### Choker

**Source** [LG:LH](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/legendary-hunters)

**Prerequisite(s)**: [Elder Voice](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/3rd-party-feats/legendary-games/elder-voice/), [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth) 4 ranks, any evil alignment

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 20 ft. climb 10 ft.; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** 2 tentacles (1d4 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores Str** 14, **Dex** 14, **Con** 11, **Int** 4, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 7; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft; **Special Attacks** [strangle](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Strangle-Ex-), [constrict](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Constrict-Ex-) (1d4)

7th-Level Advancement

**AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8 plus [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip)); **Ability Scores Str** +8, **Dex** -2, **Con** +4; **Special Qualities** quickness; **Special Attacks** [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-) (Large)

#### Dust Digger

**Note** This companion is available if the Elder Voice feat is taken. The 11th-level mastery benefit is given if the character takes the Elder Voice Mastery feat. Both can be found in Legendary Companions by Legendary Games.

**Source** [SwA:AC](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-aberration-companions-i)

**Prerequisite(s)**: Elder Voice feat

STARTING STATISTICS

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 10 ft., [burrow](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Burrow-Ex-) 20 ft.; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** bite (1d6 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)), 5 tentacles secondary [natural attack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) (1d3 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 9, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 13, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 14, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 2, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 11, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 10; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [Tremorsense](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Tremorsense-Ex-) 60 ft., +8 stealth when burrowed; **Special Attacks** [swallow whole](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Swallow-Whole-Ex-) 2d6

8th-LEVEL ADVANCEMENT

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** bite (1d8 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)), 5 tentacles secondary [natural attack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) (1d4 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +4; **Special Qualities** [Multiattack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/monster-feats/multiattack-combat); Special Attack sinkhole

Sinkhole (Ex)

A [dust digger](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/aberrations/dust-digger) can [burrow](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Burrow-Ex-) into sand, loose soil, or dirt to lie in ambush just under the surface. When it feels (via [tremorsense](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Tremorsense-Ex-)) prey walk into a square it threatens, it can deflate its body as an [immediate action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Immediate-Actions), causing the sand and other loose soil above to shift and slide. All creatures who were standing in the [dust digger](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/aberrations/dust-digger)’s reach must make a [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) save or become [entangled](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Entangled) as long as they remain in the [dust digger](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/aberrations/dust-digger)’s reach. All creatures who were standing at least partially in the [dust digger](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/aberrations/dust-digger)’s actual space must make a [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) save or become [entangled](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Entangled) and fall [prone](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Prone)—if such a creature makes this save, it immediately moves to the closest adjacent unoccupied square. If this results in more than a 5-foot move, the creature moves that [distance](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic-items/magic-weapons/magic-weapon-special-abilities/distance) and then falls [prone](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Prone). The save DC is [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-)-based.

#### Ettercap

**Source** [LG:LH](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/legendary-hunters)

**Prerequisite(s)**: [Elder Voice](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/3rd-party-feats/legendary-games/elder-voice/), [Craft](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/craft) (trapmaking) 4 ranks, any evil alignment

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 30 ft. climb 30 ft.; **Attack** bite (1d4 plus [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)) and 2 claws (1d3); **Ability Scores Str** 12, **Dex** 19, **Con** 17, **Int** 6, **Wis** 15, **Cha** 8; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), +8 [Craft](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/craft) (trapmaking); **Special Attacks** [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison) (frequency 1 round [6], effect 1d2 [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) damage, cure 2 consecutive saves, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC)

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6 plus [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)) and 2 claws (1d4); **Ability Scores Str** +2, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-)-2, **Con** +2; **Special Qualities** [spider](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/vermin/spider) empathy (HD+4) **Special Attacks** traps, [web](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/w/web) (ranged, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC, HP equal to [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-))

#### Fungal Crawler

**Note** This companion is available if the Elder Voice feat is taken. The 11th-level mastery benefit is given if the character takes the Elder Voice Mastery feat. Both can be found in Legendary Companions by Legendary Games.

**Source** [SwA:AC](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-aberration-companions-i)

**Prerequisite(s)**: Elder Voice feat

STARTING STATISTICS

**Size** Small; **Speed** 20 ft., climb 40 ft.; **Attack(s)** bite (1d6 plus [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)), 2 claws (1d4); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 14, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 20 [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 15, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 2, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 13, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 7; **Special Qualities** [plant](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Plant) defenses

8th-LEVEL ADVANCEMENT

**Special Attacks**

Leap (Ex)

A crawler can perform a special kind of [pounce](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Pounce-Ex-) attack by jumping into combat. When a crawler charges, it can make a DC 20 [Acrobatics](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/acrobatics) check to jump into the air and land next to its enemies. If it makes the [Acrobatics](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/acrobatics) check, it can follow up with four claw attacks against foes in reach, but it cannot make a bite attack.

Plant Defenses (Ex)

A crawler is part [plant](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Plant) and shares many of the immunities that [plant](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Plant) creatures possess. A crawler is immune to [mind-affecting](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic#TOC-Magic-Descriptor-Mind-Affecting) effects, [paralysis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Paralysis), [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison), [polymorph](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/p/polymorph), [sleep](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/s/sleep), and stunning.

Poison (Ex)

Bite—injury; *save* [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude), [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC; *frequency* 1/round for 4 rounds; *effect* 1d2 [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) and 1d2 [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-); *cure* 1 save.

#### Geomaw

**Source** [SwA:AC](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-aberration-companions-i)

**Note** This companion is available if the Elder Voice feat is taken. The 11th-level mastery benefit is given if the character takes the Elder Voice Mastery feat. Both can be found in Legendary Companions by Legendary Games.

**Prerequisite(s)**: Elder Voice feat, [Great Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/great-fortitude)

STARTING STATISTICS

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 10 ft., [burrow](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Burrow-Ex-) 20 ft.; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** bite (2d4); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 16, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 9, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 16, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 6, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 11, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 13; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [tremorsense](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Tremorsense-Ex-) 60ft., [blind](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Blinded), blood gorger, [freeze](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Freeze-Ex-);Special Attacks [swallow whole](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Swallow-Whole-Ex-) (2d6 and 2d6 acid)

9th-LEVEL ADVANCEMENT

**Size** Large; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** bite (2d6); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +4

MASTERY (11th-Level)

**Special Attacks** blood lantern

Blood Gorger (Ex)

An enraged [remorhaz](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/remorhaz) generates [heat](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Heat-Ex-) so intense that anything touching its body takes 4d6 points of fire damage. Creatures striking a [remorhaz](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/remorhaz) with [natural attacks](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) or unarmed strikes are subject to this damage, but not creatures striking with melee weapons. The [heat](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Heat-Ex-) can melt or burn weapons any weapon that strikes a [remorhaz](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/remorhaz) is allowed a DC 19 [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) save to avoid taking damage. The save DC is [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based.

Freeze (Ex)

While lying motionless with its mouth open, a geomaw appears to be a [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus) crystal formation. A geomaw that uses [freeze](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Freeze-Ex-) can [take 20](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Take-20) on its [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth) check to [hide in plain sight](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/rogue/rogue-talents/paizo---rogue-advanced-talents/hide-in-plain-sight-ex) as a [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus) cave feature.

Blood Lantern (Su)

As a [swift action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Swift-Actions) in any round it inflicts damage to a victim it has swallowed whole, a geomaw can emit a [scintillating pattern](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/s/scintillating-pattern) of red-hued [light](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/l/light) from its crystalline interior. All creatures within 30 feet must succeed at a [Will](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Will) saving throw or be [fascinated](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Fascinated). This is a sight-based, [mind-affecting](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic#TOC-Magic-Descriptor-Mind-Affecting) [compulsion](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic#TOC-Enchantment-Compulsion) effect. A creature that successfully saves cannot be affected by the same geomaw’s blood [lantern](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/equipment/goods-and-services/hunting-camping-survival-gear#TOC-Lantern) for 24 hours. The save DC is [Charisma](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-)-based.

#### Lunarma

**Prerequisite(s)**: Elder Voice feat, [Great Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/great-fortitude)

STARTING STATISTICS

**Size** Small; **Speed** 0 ft., fly 60 ft. (good); **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** 3 claws (1d6 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)), bite (1d4); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 12, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 14, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 17, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 5, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 12, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 10; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., barbed carapace, [no breath](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-No-Breath-Ex-); [CMB](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Combat-Maneuver-Bonus) +4 [grapple](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple); **Special Attacks** [constrict](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Constrict-Ex-) (1d6)

9th-LEVEL ADVANCEMENT

**Size** Medium; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** 3 claws (1d8 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)), bite (1d8); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +4, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2

MASTERY (11th-Level)

Barbed Carapace (Ex)

A lunarma’s carapace is covered in jagged barbs. Any creature that grapples a lunarma or attacks it with unarmed strikes or [natural weapons](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) takes 1d4 (1d3 when it is Small) points of damage from the [vicious](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic-items/magic-weapons/magic-weapon-special-abilities/vicious) barbs. Using a reach weapon does not endanger the attacker this way.

Breath Weapon (Su)

30-ft. line, 2d6 acid damage plus recurring damage, [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) half, usable every 1d4 rounds.

The acid from a lunarma’s [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) lasts for 1d4 additional rounds, dealing 2d6 points of acid damage on its turn to any creature that took damage from the [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-). Washing off the acid with water or other liquid is a [full-round action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Full-Round-Actions) that ends the continuing damage.

#### Reefclaw

**Prerequisite(s)**: Elder Voice feat

STARTING STATISTICS

**Size** Small; **Speed** 5 ft., swim 40 ft.; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack(s)** 2 claws (1d4 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-) and [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 10, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 13, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 14, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 5, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 12, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 11; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent), racial skill bonus: +8 [Swim](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/swim), [ferocity](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Ferocity-Ex-); **CMD** can’t be [tripped](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip).; **Resist** cold 5; **Special Attacks** death frenzy, [constrict](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Constrict-Ex-) (1d4)

9th-LEVEL ADVANCEMENT

**Size** Medium; **Attack(s)** 2 claws (1d6 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-) and [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +4, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2

Death Frenzy (Ex)

When killed, the reefclaw spasms horribly making a full attack as an [immediate action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Immediate-Actions) against a creature it threatens. If more than one creature is within reach, roll randomly for the target of each attack.

Grab (Ex)

A reefclaw can [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-) targets of any size, and has a +8 [racial bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Racial-Bonus) on [grapple](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple) checks rather than the normal +4 bonus.

Poison (Ex)

Claw-injury; *save* fortitude, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC; *frequency* 1/round for 4 rounds; *effect* 1d2 [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) damage; *cure* 1 save

#### Tearjerker

**Size** Small; **Speed** 20 ft., climb 20 ft.; **Attack(s)** 2 talons (1d4); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 7, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 17, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 12, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 2, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 14, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 11; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [All-around vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-All-Around-Vision-Ex-); **Special Attacks** blinding [stench](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Stench-Ex-)

7th-LEVEL ADVANCEMENT

**Special Attacks**: devour the eyes of the soul

Blinding Stench (Ex)

Tearjerkers exude a toxic musk that stinks of bleach. This ability functions identically to the [stench](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Stench-Ex-) ability, save that a creature that fails its saving throw is [blinded](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Blinded) rather than [nauseated](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Nauseated) for the effect’s duration. Already [blind](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Blinded), or eyeless creatures are unaffected.

Devour the Eyes of the Soul (Su)

Tearjerkers eat the eyes of their victims before any other part of the anatomy. A creature whose eyes are devoured by a tearjerker remains permanently [blinded](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Blinded) even if returned to life by [raise dead](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/r/raise-dead). It requires [true resurrection](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/t/true-resurrection), [restoration](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/r/restoration) or other powerful magic to restore sight to a creature slain by a tearjerker.

#### Tentamort

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Speed** 20 ft., climb 20 ft.; **Attack** sting (1d4 plus [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)) and [tentacle](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/base-classes/alchemist/discoveries/paizo---alchemist-discoveries/tentacle-ex) (1d4 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-)** 13, **Dex** 15, **Con** 12, **Int** 1, **Wis** 14, **Cha** 6; **Special Qualities** [all-around vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-All-Around-Vision-Ex-), [blindsense](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Blindsight-and-Blindsense) 30 ft., [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft.; **Special Attacks** [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison) (frequency 2 rounds, effect 1d4 [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) damage plus nausea, cure 1 save, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC), [constrict](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Constrict-Ex-) (1d4)

### Accursed Companions

When a character calls upon the aid and companionship of one of nature’s children, she forges a sacred pact to care for and cherish that creature. In exchange, the animal companion serves as her guide and guardian.

The bond between the two strengthens, and the animal companion moves beyond its primal instincts and its soul blossoms. This transcendence is both beautiful and wondrous, but as with all magic, there is always a cost.

As an animal companion’s consciousness grows, it can sometimes attract the attention of the spiritual energies that hide in plain sight everywhere. While some of these forces are good or indifferent, others lurk in the void, in the deepest shadows where death waits. When the right moment comes, these darker entities latch onto these proud companions with a vicious hunger. Should the character fail to protect her companion, corruption ebbs forth and fills the once-magnificent creatures with vile intent. Cursed and corrupted, these companions return to their masters broken, scarred, and distraught. Theirs is a curse they are bound to share, for when mortals fail to protect their bonded companions, so too shall those mortals suffer.

When a cavalier, druid, hunter, ranger, or other character loses an animal companion to a disturbingly gruesome death, particularly if that fate could have been avoided through an act the character chose not to or was unable to take, the soul of the slain animal companion sometimes remains bound to the character. In such cases, this scarred soul infests the next companion the character takes.

### Gaining an Accursed Companion

Any character with the animal companion or mount class ability can choose to gain an accursed animal companion once a previous animal companion has suffered a violent, humiliating, or particularly horrible death. The character must then choose to gain an accursed companion while performing the ritual to replace the slain companion. At the GM’s discretion, the player might automatically gain an accursed companion unless she takes the time to seek atonement for allowing her previous companion to die.

### Accursed Companion Manifestations

An accursed companion’s unnatural condition manifests in one of the following ways, chosen at the time the companion is gained. Once selected, the choice cannot be changed. Who gets to choose the manifestation depends on the GM’s preference (the manifestation may even be randomly determined).

All manifestations grant a boon in combat to the animal companion but a disadvantage to the master. An animal companion’s accursed manifestation can be activated in one of two ways: the companion’s master can deliberately trigger a manifestation by making a successful DC 20 Handle Animal or wild empathy check as a move action, or the manifestation can take place when a specific trigger occurs, as detailed in each manifestation’s entry.

When an accursed companion manifests its condition, the companion’s master can resist or mitigate the debilitating side effect with a successful Will save (DC = 10 + 1/2 the accursed companion’s HD + the accursed companion’s Wisdom modifier [minimum +0]). However, manifestations that are constant (such as festering flesh or unsavory friends) have an equally constant effect on the companion’s master, and these effects cannot be mitigated or resisted in any way. An accursed companion can only be affected by a manifestation once per hour unless the manifestation is constant. All side effects on an accursed companion’s master are mind-affecting effects.

#### Bestial Flashes (Su)

The companion is haunted by the previous companion’s fear and pain during its death.

This manifestation is triggered automatically whenever the accursed companion takes damage from a single blow in excess of half its current hit points. When an accursed companion suffers bestial flashes, it gains a +2 morale bonus on all attack rolls and damage rolls made on natural attacks, and gains a +4 morale bonus on rolls to confirm critical hits. Once triggered, a bestial flash lasts for 1 minute. When a bestial flash occurs, the mind of the companion’s master is overwhelmed with images of feral savagery. She becomes confused for 1d4 rounds and is then sickened for the remainder of the minute that the bestial flash persists. On a successful Will save, the master is instead sickened for only 1d4 rounds.

#### Bloodthirsty (Su)

The companion becomes consumed with bloodlust that drives it into a frenzy of savage ferocity. This manifestation is triggered automatically whenever the accursed companion makes a successful critical hit with a natural attack. When the companion becomes bloodthirsty, it flies into a rage and gains +2 Constitution and +2 Strength, but it also takes a –2 penalty to its AC. The rage lasts until the battle is over or for 1 minute, whichever is shorter. It cannot end its rage voluntarily. The companion’s master is overwhelmed with rage as well for this period, although this rage is unfocused and distracting, preventing the master from doing anything but growling, hissing, shrieking, and making other animalistic howls, during which time the master cannot speak or use spells with verbal components. A successful Will save reduces the duration of the master’s rage to 1 round.

#### Festering Flesh (Su)

The companion looks horrific and smells worse. Its rancid flesh reeks of rot and crawls with fleas, ticks, and other vile parasites. Despite its obvious grotesqueness, the creature is quite affectionate, perhaps even overly and inappropriately so. This manifestation is always active—the accursed companion is immune to the sickened and nauseated condition. The master, on the other hand, becomes consumed by fears of contagion to the extent that she takes a –2 penalty on all saving throws against disease effects.

#### Palsy (Su)

The poor creature is stricken with palsy.

It drools constantly and its muscles spasm with tics and twitches. The palsy doesn’t impact its abilities, and actually aids the accursed companion when it loses mobility from other sources. The first time each day that the accursed companion becomes paralyzed, grappled or otherwise has its movement impaired, a freedom of movement effect automatically activates on the accursed companion. This effect persists for 1 minute, during which time the companion’s master becomes nauseated unless she succeeds at a Will save (in which case she is merely sickened for the duration).

#### Rabid Vomit (Ex)

A crust of froth lines the rim of the accursed companion’s mouth. This manifestation is triggered automatically on the third round of any combat—on this round, the accursed companion always takes a standard action to vomit diseased pus and bile in a 15-foot cone (after moving, if it can, to capture as many enemies in the area of effect as possible). All creatures in this area must succeed at a [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat/#TOC-Fortitude) saving throw (DC = 10 + 1/2 the accursed companion’s HD + the accursed companion’s Constitution modifier) or become nauseated for 1d4 rounds and contract rabies. On a successful save, the targets are merely sickened for 1d4 rounds. When the accursed companion makes this vomit attack, its master is overwhelmed by the sensation of a mouthful of diseased bile. She is stunned for 1 round and nauseated for 1d4 rounds thereafter unless she succeeds at a Will save, in which case she is merely sickened for 1d4 rounds.

#### Scavenger (Su)

This companion is particularly intrigued by undeath, often playing with carcasses and presenting decaying body parts as gifts to its master. This manifestation is triggered automatically when the companion successfully damages a corporeal undead with a natural attack. For 1 minute, the companion gains a +2 bonus on all attack rolls, damage rolls, and saving throws against undead. During this time, the companion’s master becomes more susceptible to the undead, and takes a –2 penalty to all mind-affecting effects created by any undead creature.

#### Unexpected Frenzy (Su)

The accursed companion looks normal, but some conditions or phrases cause the animal to fly into a murderous frenzy. When an accursed companion gains this condition, the GM determines three specific situations that can trigger the manifestation of the unexpected frenzy, such as a character petting the companion on the head, a keyword or key phrase such as “good dog,” or the sight of a specific type of creature within 10 feet. The first time each day one of the three triggers occurs, the accursed companion flies into its frenzy. Its eyes glow, and any sounds it makes take on an eerie, hollow echo. The companion acts as if under the effects of haste for 1d4 rounds before returning to normal, and it typically attacks the source of its trigger. While her companion is frenzied, the master is overwhelmed with shame and despair, suffering as if under the effects of a crushing despair spell for twice the length of the accursed companion’s frenzy. A successful Will save negates this effect.

#### Unsavory Friends (Su)

The companion manages to attract the company of less desirable species. It has an uncanny knack for finding centipedes, bats, mice, and other vermin, even in areas where such pests might not be all that common. Even more unusual, the companion makes it a habit to play with such creatures and becomes angry and defensive if anything threatens its vermin friends. This manifestation is constant.

Immune to the distraction effect caused by all swarms, the animal companion is comfortable and even welcomes the nauseating sensation of its crawling friends. The companion’s master, unfortunately, never gets used to finding squirming bugs or wriggling maggots in the companion’s vicinity and takes a –4 penalty on all saving throws against any swarm’s distraction ability.

### Magical Beast Companions

The following creatures can be chosen as Magical Beast companions by a character with [the Beast Speaker feat](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/beast-speaker/). Their entries and advancement are the same as for [animal companions](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid/animal-companions), with two exceptions. First, creatures with an [Intelligence](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) score of 3 or higher have one or more additional prerequisites the character must meet to select the companion. Second, each beast companion has a mastery ability that it can use only if the character it is bonded to has the [Beast Speaker Mastery feat](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/beast-speaker-mastery/). The minimum level to gain this ability is listed in parentheses. The save DC for any of a beast companion’s special abilities is 10 + half the beast companion’s HD + the beast companion’s [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) modifier.

#### Basilisk

**Source** [PPC:HoG](https://amzn.to/2XWCEyw)

Starting Statistics

**Size**: Medium; **Speed** 20 ft.; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d4); **Ability Scores** **Str** 16, **Dex** 10, **Con** 15, **Int** 2, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 11; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Low-Light-Vision-Ex-), [gaze](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Gaze-Su-) (one target within 30 ft., [paralysis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Paralysis) 1d4 rounds, [Fort](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) negates, once per day).

9th-Level Advancement

**AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Ability Scores** [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) +4, **Con** +4; **Attack** bite (1d6); **Special Qualities** [gaze](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Gaze-Su-) (three times per day).

Mastery (11th level)

**Size** The [basilisk’s](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/basilisk) [gaze](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Gaze-Su-) attack functions as [flesh to stone](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/f/flesh-to-stone) ([caster level](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic#TOC-Caster-Level) equals [basilisk’s](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/basilisk) HD) instead of inflicting [paralysis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Paralysis).

#### Behir

**Source** [PPC:HoG](https://amzn.to/2XWCEyw)

**Prerequisite(s)**: [Diplomacy](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/diplomacy) or [Intimidate](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/intimidate) 7 ranks, [Knowledge](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/knowledge) (arcana) 7 ranks.

Starting Statistics

**Size**: Medium; **Speed** 40 ft., climb 20 ft.; **AC** +6 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** 16, **Dex** 12, **Con** 16, **Int** 7, **Wis** 14, **Cha** 12; **Special Attacks** [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) (20-ft. line, 4d6 electricity damage, [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) half, once per day), [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-); **Special Qualities** [electricity resistance](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Energy-Resistance) 10.

Mastery (11th level)

**Size:**  Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** –2, **Con** +2; **Special Attacks** [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) (three times per day), [constrict](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Constrict-Ex-) 1d8; **Special Qualities** immune to electricity.

#### Bulette

**Source** [PPC:HoG](https://amzn.to/2XWCEyw)

Starting Statistics

**Size**: Medium; **Speed** 40 ft., [burrow](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Burrow-Ex-) 20 ft.; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6), 2 claws (1d4); **Ability Scores** **Str** 16, **Dex** 14, **Con** 16, **Int** 2, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 6.

Mastery (11th level)

**Size** Large; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8), claws (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** –2, **Con** +2; **Special Attacks** leap (When charging, it can attempt a DC 20 [Acrobatics](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/acrobatics) check to jump into the air and land next to its enemies. If successful, it can make four claw attacks against foes in reach but cannot make a bite attack).

#### Bunyip

Starting Statistics

[[Source](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-magical-beast-companions-ii)])

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 10 ft., swim 50 ft.; **Attack** bite (1d8 plus [bleed](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Bleed)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 12, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 16, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 13, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 2, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 11, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 7; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [keen scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Keen-Scent-Ex-) 120 ft.; **Special Attacks** [bleed](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Bleed) (1d6)

8th-Level Advancement

**AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Special Attacks** [blood rage](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/b/blood-rage), roar

Blood Rage (Ex)

A [bunyip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/bunyip)’s [blood rage](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/b/blood-rage) ability activates whenever it detects blood in the water using its [keen scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Keen-Scent-Ex-), but otherwise functions as the universal monster rule of the same name.

Roar (Su)

A [bunyip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/bunyip)’s roar is supernaturally loud and horrifying. When a [bunyip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/bunyip) roars (a [standard action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Standard-Actions) the creature can perform at will), all hearing creatures with 4 or fewer HD within a 100-foot spread must succeed on a DC [Will](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Will) save or become [panicked](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Panicked) for 2d4 rounds. Whether or not the save is successful, creatures in the area are immune to the roar of that [bunyip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/bunyip) for 24 hours. This is a sonic, [mind-affecting](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic#TOC-Magic-Descriptor-Mind-Affecting) [fear](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Fear) effect. The save DC is [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based.

**Size** Tiny; **Speed** 30 ft., fly 80 ft. (average); **Attack** bite (1d3) and 2 claws (1d2); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 6, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 17, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 11, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 2, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 14, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 7; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent), [Perception](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/perception) +3 on sight-based checks, +4 [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth)

#### Catoblepas

**Prerequisite(s)**: base [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) bonus +4

Starting Statistics

[[Source](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-magical-beast-companions-ii)])

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 40 ft., swim 20 ft.; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d10), gore (1d8), 2 hooves (1d6); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 12, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 10, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 18, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 5, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 15, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 10; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision); **Special Attacks** [stench](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Stench-Ex-) (10 feet)

9th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (2d8), gore (2d6), 2 hooves (1d8); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +4; **Special Attacks** [stench](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Stench-Ex-) (20 feet) Mastery (11th-Level)
**Special Attacks** [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison) breath, [stench](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Stench-Ex-) (30 feet)

Poison Breath (Ex)

A [catoblepas](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/catoblepas)’s horrid, stinking breath is 60-foot cone of [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison) gas. This [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) is usable once every 1d6 rounds. The save DC is [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based.

**Breath**—contact; *save* [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude); *frequency* 1/round for 6 rounds; *effect* 1d4 [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) damage; *cure* 2 consecutive saves.

Stench (Ex)

This functions as the universal monster ability, has a radius detailed above, and the DC is [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based. The character is not affected by their own [catoblepas](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/catoblepas)’s [stench](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Stench-Ex-).

#### Frost-Ferret

Starting Statistics

[[Source](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-magical-beast-companions-ii)])

**Size** Tiny; **Speed** 20 ft., climb 20 ft.; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d3); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 3, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 16, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 10, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 2, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 12, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 5; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent), [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth) +4, [Acrobatics](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/acrobatics) +8; Immune cold; **Special Attacks** [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) (2d6, 15 ft)

9th-Level Advancement

**Size** Small; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d4); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +4, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2; **Special Attacks** [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) (4d6, 20 ft)

Breath Weapon (Su)

A [frost](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic-items/magic-weapons/magic-weapon-special-abilities/frost)-ferret’s [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) deals the listed amount in cold damage in a cone. The length of the cone is listed in the entry above.

The [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) is usable once every 1d4 rounds, and allows a [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) save for half damage. The save DC is [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based.

#### Hippogriff

**Source** [LG:LH](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/legendary-hunters)

**Prerequisite(s)**: [Beast-Speaker](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/beast-speaker/)

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 10 ft., fly 100 ft. #### Manticore

**Source** [LG:LH](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/legendary-hunters)

#### Maw

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; Speed 20 ft.; AC +4 [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); Attack bite (1d8) or claw (1d3); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 12, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 12, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 14, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 1, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 12, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 2; Special Qualities +4 saves vs. [disease](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/diseases) and [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)

7th-level Advancement

**Size** Medium; AC +2 [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); Attack bite (1d10 plus [disease](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/diseases)) or claw (1d4); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +4, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2

Disease (red ache)

Bite-injury; *save* [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude), [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC; *onset* 1d3 days; *frequency* 1/day; *effect* 1d6 [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) damage; *cure* 2 consecutive saves

#### Mule-Lizard

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; Speed 20 ft.; AC +2 [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); Attack bite (1d4); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 12, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 12, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 14, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 1, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 12, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 2; Special Qualities [Low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Low-Light-Vision-Ex-), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent), [adaptive](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic-items/magic-weapons/magic-weapon-special-abilities/adaptive) [camouflage](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/rogue/rogue-talents/paizo---rogue-talents/camouflage-ex), strong-legged

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; Attack bite (1d8); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +4, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2

Adaptive Camouflage (Ex)

If given 8 hours in a new environment, the mule-lizard can changed the colors and patterns in its skin to grant itself a +4 bonus on [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth) checks. Alternatively, the master of the mule lizard can provoke it to take on more flamboyant colors, basically taking on patterns and colors of the master’s choice but they lose the [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth) bonus.

#### Strong-legged (Ex)

The mule-lizard is bipedal but has [stable](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Stable), strong legs. They gain a +4 bonus on their [CMD](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Combat-Maneuver-Defense) vs. bull-rush and [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip). Additionally, they may carry loads as if they were a quadruped and may carry riders up to their size.

(average; the [pegasus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/pegasus) can carry a rider while flying, but reduces its fly speed by half while doing so.); **Attack bite (1d4), 2 hooves (1d6, primary [natural attack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks)); Ability Scores [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2.****

#### Qiongqi

**Prerequisite(s)**: [Chaotic](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Chaotic) [Evil](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Evil), [Bluff](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/bluff) 5 ranks

Starting Statistics

[[Source](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-magical-beast-companions-ii)])

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 40 ft. [fly](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/f/fly) 120 ft. (average) ; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)) and 2 claws (1d6 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 15, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 17, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 13, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 10, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 12, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 10; **Special Qualities** [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent), racial skill bonus +8 [Bluff](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/bluff), +4 [Acrobatics](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/acrobatics), [sound mimicry](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Sound-Mimicry-Ex-) (voices); **CMB** +4 [grapple](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple)

9th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (2d6 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)) and 2 claws (1d8 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +4; **Special Qualities** [pounce](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Pounce-Ex-), [rake](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Rake-Ex-) (2 claws 1d8)

Sound Mimicry (Ex)

The creature perfectly imitates certain sounds or even specific voices. The creature attempts a [Bluff](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/bluff) check opposed by the listener’s [Sense Motive](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/sense-motive) check to recognize the mimicry, although if the listener isn’t [familiar](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/animals/familiar) with the person or type of creatures mimicked, it takes a –8 penalty on its [Sense Motive](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/sense-motive) check. The creature has a +8 [racial bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Racial-Bonus) on its [Bluff](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/bluff) check to mimic sounds (including accents and speech patterns, if a voice mimic) it has listened to for at least 10 minutes. The creature cannot duplicate the effects of magical abilities (such as [bardic performance](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/bard#TOC-Bardic-Performance) or a [harpy](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/monstrous-humanoids/harpy)’s captivating song), though it may be able to mimic the sound of those abilities. This ability does not allow the creature to speak or understand languages it doesn’t know.

#### Ridge Flier

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; Speed 10 ft., fly 80 ft. (average); AC +1 [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); Attack bite (1d4); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 12, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 17, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 12, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) 1, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 14, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 10; Special Qualities [Low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Low-Light-Vision-Ex-), sense intruder, hyper-aggression racial skill bonus: +4 [Perception](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/perception)

4th-Level Advancement

**AC** +1 [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +2

Sense Intruder (Ex)

Ridge fliers have a preternatural ability to sense when a creature has entered their territory. A ridge flier gains a +20 bonus to [Perception](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/perception) checks to notice the presence of a creature nearby. This only allows them to know there is a creature within 100 feet of them, they must make a standard [Perception](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/perception) check (without the bonus) to pinpoint the intruder.

#### Hyper-aggression (Ex)

If a ridge flier can see a creature that they do not recognize as part of their flock or other individual they are trained to accept, there is a 10% chance every minute that they will [fly](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/f/fly) into a [rage](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/r/rage) and attack the invading creature. The ridge flier gains a +2 bonus to [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) and [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-), a +8 bonus to [Perception](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/perception) to find the target of its [rage](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/r/rage), and a -2 penalty to its AC. The [rage](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/r/rage) lasts until the creature is [dead](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Dead) or 1 minute, whichever is shorter. The ridge flier cannot end this [rage](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/r/rage) voluntarily.

If the ridge flier enters a combat not already under the effects of the hyper-aggression, or the original target is killed during the combat, the chance that the ridge flier enters the [rage](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/r/rage) is increased to 50% each round. The combat-induced [rage](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/r/rage) is directed at a random qualifying target in sight.
