#### Sun Falcon

**Source** [PPC:HoG](https://amzn.to/2XWCEyw)

**Prerequisite(s)**: [Diplomacy](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/diplomacy) 7 ranks, [Knowledge](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/knowledge) (arcana) or [Knowledge](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/knowledge) (religion) 7 ranks.

Starting Statistics

**Size**: Tiny; **Speed** 10 ft., fly 60 ft. (good); **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** talons (1d4 plus burn); **Ability Scores** **Str** 10, **Dex** 17, **Con** 12, **Int** 5, **Wis** 14, **Cha** 15; **Special Attacks** [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) (30-ft. line, 3d6 fire, [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) half, once per day), burn (1d4).

9th-Level Advancement

Size Small; **AC** 19 +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** talons (1d6 plus burn); **Ability Scores** **Str** +2, **Con** +4, **Cha** +2; **Special Attacks** [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) (three times per day), burn (1d6).

Mastery (11th level)

**Size** Three times per day, the sun falcon can blast an intense wave of heat and light in a 20-foot cone as a [standard action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Standard-Actions). Creatures within this area must succeed at a [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) save or take 1d6 points of fire damage and be [blinded](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Blinded) for 1d4+1 rounds. Creatures that succeed at this save take no fire damage and are instead [dazzled](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Dazzled) for 1 round. The save DC is [Charisma](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-)-based.

#### Trollhound

Starting Statistics

[[Source](https://www.opengamingstore.com/products/speak-with-animals-magical-beast-companions-ii)])

Otherworldly Touch (Ex)

A zoog’s [natural attacks](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) can strike [incorporeal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Incorporeal) creatures as if they were [ghost touch](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic-items/magic-weapons/magic-weapon-special-abilities/ghost-touch) weapons.

### Other Magical Beast Companions

The following creatures can be chosen as Magical Beast companions by a character with the [Monstrous Mount](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/monstrous-mount/) feat. Their entries and advancement are the same as for [animal companions](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid/animal-companions), with two exceptions. First, creatures with an [Intelligence](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) score of 3 or higher have one or more additional prerequisites the character must meet to select the companion. Second, each beast companion has a mastery ability that it can use only if the character it is bonded to has the [Monstrous Mount Mastery](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/monstrous-mount-mastery/) feat. The minimum level to gain this ability is listed in parentheses. The save DC for any of a beast companion’s special abilities is 10 + half the beast companion’s HD + the beast companion’s [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) modifier.

#### Griffon

**Prerequisite(s)**: [Diplomacy](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/diplomacy), [Intimidate](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/intimidate), or [Handle Animal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/handle-animal) 5 ranks; [Ride](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/ride) 5 ranks.

Starting Statistics

**Size** Large; **Speed** 30 ft., fly 40 ft. (average; unable to carry a rider while flying); **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6); **Ability Scores Str** 16, **Dex** 15, **Con** 16, **Int** 5, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 8; **Languages** Common (cannot speak); **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent).

7th-Level Advancement

**Speed** 40 ft., fly 80 ft. (average; unable to carry a rider while flying); **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6), 2 talons (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** +2, **Con** +2; **Special Attacks** [pounce](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Pounce-Ex-), [rake](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Rake-Ex-) (1d6).

Mastery (7th Level)

The griffon can carry a rider while flying, but reduces its fly speed by half while doing so.

The hippocampus’s swim speed increases by 20 feet, and it gains a tail slap secondary attack that deals 1d4 points of damage plus half its [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) bonus.

#### Worg

**Prerequisite(s)**: Alignment within one step of neutral evil.

Mastery (7th Level)

Once per day as a [standard action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Standard-Actions), the worg can make a fearful howl. This functions as the [fear](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Fear) cone (30 ft.) version of the [fear](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Fear) universal monster rule.

### Plant Companions

**Prerequisite(s)** To gain a plant companion the druid must be an elf and possess the [treesinger druid archetype](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/races/core-races/elf/treesinger-druid-elf).

Each plant companion has different starting sizes, speed, attacks, ability scores, and special qualities. All plant attacks are made using the creature’s full [base attack bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Attack-Bonus) unless otherwise noted. Plant attacks add the [plant’s](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Plant) [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/cleric/domains/paizo-domains/strength-domain) modifier on the damage roll, unless it has only one attack, in which case it adds 1-1/2 times its [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/cleric/domains/paizo-domains/strength-domain) modifier. Some plant companions have special abilities, such as [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent). Plant companions cannot gain armor or weapon proficiency feats, even as they advance in hit dice, and cannot use manufactured weapons at all unless their description says otherwise.

As you gain levels, your plant companion grows in power as well. It gains the same bonuses that are gained by [animal companions](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid/animal-companions/animal-companions), noted on **Table: Animal Companion Base Statistics**. Each plant companion gains an additional bonus, usually at 4th or 7th level, as listed with each plant choice. Instead of taking the listed benefit at 4th level, you can instead choose to increase the companion’s [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/cleric/domains/paizo-domains/strength-domain) and [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) by 2.

This surprisingly mobile, multicolored ball of fungus crawls around on a nest of dozens of little filament-like “legs.” Its poisonous spores cause those affected to endure bright, dazzling spots of color.

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 30 ft.; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** slam (1d4 plus [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)); **Ability Scores** **Str** 12, **Dex** 15, **Con** 14, **Int** 1, **Wis** 12, **Cha** 9; **Special Attacks** [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison) (frequency 1 round [4]; *effect* 1d2 [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) damage and [dazzled](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Dazzled); *cure* 1 save; [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC); **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., defensive puff (1/minute as an [immediate action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Immediate-Actions) when hit, the fungus can expose one adjacent creature to its [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)); **CMD** can’t be [tripped](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip).

4th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** slam (1d6 plus [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** –2, **Con** +2.

#### Gulper Plant

[[Source](http://amzn.to/2z71S07)]

This bulbous green [plant](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Plant) can climb or crawl via a network of vines. Its central reservoir can gulp down foes to digest them in an internal well of acid, holding them tight while they struggle.

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 20 ft., climb 10 ft.; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** 2 vines (1d4 plus [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** **Str** 12, **Dex** 11, **Con** 13, **Int** 1, **Wis** 10, **Cha** 3; **Special Attacks** [swallow whole](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Swallow-Whole-Ex-) (1d6 acid); **Special Qualities** [freeze](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Freeze-Ex-), [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision); **CMD** can’t be [tripped](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip).

7th-Level Advancement

This attack is a primary [natural attack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) that deals bludgeoning damage.

### Vermin Companions

**Source**: [PZO1117](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1601252994/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_il_tl?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1601252994&linkCode=as2&tag=httpwwwd20pfs-20 "PZO1117")

Vermin companions follow the same rules as animal companions, advancing their [Hit Dice](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Hit-Dice-HD-) and other abilities per Table: Animal Companion Base Statistics. Vermin companions can be trained as if they were [animals](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Animal) using the [Handle Animal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/handle-animal) skill.

**Mindless**: [Vermin](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Vermin) companions have no [Intelligence](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) score and possess the mindless trait. In spite of this, vermin companions may learn one trick, plus additional bonus tricks as noted on Table: Animal Companion Base Statistics. If a [vermin](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Vermin) animal companion gains an ability score increase (at 4 [Hit Dice](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Hit-Dice-HD-), 8 [Hit Dice](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Hit-Dice-HD-), and so on), the [druid](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/core-classes/druid) can apply this increase to the companion’s [Intelligence](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-), changing it from — to 1, at which point the companion loses the mindless quality and is able to know up to 3 tricks per point of [Intelligence](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-), plus the additional bonus tricks, as per [Handle Animal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/handle-animal). [Vermin](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Vermin) companions have no skill points or feats as long as they have the mindless quality.

**Trip**: Because many vermin have multiple limbs, they are very difficult to [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip). As a result, a [CMD](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Combat-Maneuver-Defense) entry has been included for each, indicating the bonus to [CMD](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Combat-Maneuver-Defense) such vermin receive against [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip) attacks.

The long thin tendrils that lash out from this [centipede’s](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/vermin/centipede) tail can [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip) foes with surprising ease.

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 40 ft., climb 40 ft.; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6 plus [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)); **Ability Scores** **Str** 9, **Dex** 13, **Con** 13, **Int** —, **Wis** 10, **Cha** 2; **Special Attacks** [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison) (frequency 1 round [4]; *effect* 1d2 **Dex** damage; *cure* 1 save; [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC); **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft.; **CMD** can’t be [tripped](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip).

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8 plus [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison)), tail slap (1d2 [nonlethal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Nonlethal-Damage) plus [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip)); **Ability Scores** **Str** +8, **Dex** –2, **Con** +4.

This attack gains no bonus from the creature’s [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) score on damage rolls.

#### Thundercloud Jellyfish

**Requirement** the the Beast Speaker feat

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** fly 20 ft. (perfect); AC +2 [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); Attack [tentacle](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/base-classes/alchemist/discoveries/paizo---alchemist-discoveries/tentacle-ex) melee [touch](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Touch-Attacks) (1d6 electricity plus [paralysis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Paralysis)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) 6, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) 12, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) 14, [Int](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Intelligence-Int-) -, [Wis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Wisdom-Wis-) 12, [Cha](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) 1; Special Attacks [paralysis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Paralysis) (Conbased DC); Special Qualities [blindsight](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Blindsight-and-Blindsense) 60 feet, [blind](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Blinded), [amorphous](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Amorphous-Ex-), shocking tentacles; [DR](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Damage-Reduction-Ex-or-Su-) 10/slashing or piercing; [CMD](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Combat-Maneuver-Defense) cannot be [tripped](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip)

7th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; AC +2 [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); Attack [tentacle](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/classes/base-classes/alchemist/discoveries/paizo---alchemist-discoveries/tentacle-ex) melee [touch](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Touch-Attacks) (1d8 electricity plus [paralysis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Paralysis)); **Ability Scores** [Str](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) +8, [Dex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Dexterity-Dex-) -2, [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) +4

Shocking Tentacles (Ex)

A thundercloud jellyfish’s arms deliver electricity damage and a [paralysis](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Paralysis) *effect* with a melee [touch attack](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Touch-Attacks). The creature’s [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) modifier is used for the [attack roll](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Attack-Roll) but is not added to damage. Additionally, when large size, the arms have a 10-foot reach. The arms are unable to [grapple](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple) unless the target creature is 3 size categories smaller than the thundercloud [Jellyfish](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/vermin/jellyfish). The arms are predominantly for bringing [plant](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Plant) material to the mouth within the bell, not for picking up or wrapping around larger foes.

#### Mosquito, Giant

[[Source](http://amzn.to/2z71S07)]

Between its bloodthirsty nature and the annoying drone of its wings, the giant mosquito is a much-loathed creature. Unlike its smaller cousins, a [giant mosquito](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/vermin/mosquito-giant) can easily kill larger creatures by draining them of their blood.

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 20 ft., fly 60 ft. (good); **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6 plus [bleed](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Bleed) and [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-)); **Ability Scores** **Str** 14, **Dex** 21, **Con** 15, **Int** —, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 6; **Special Attacks** [bleed](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Bleed) (1d4), [grab](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Grab-Ex-); **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft.; **CMD** +8 vs. [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip).
