4th-Level Advancement

**Ability Scores** **Str** +2, **Int** +2; **Special Qualities** [combat trained](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/handle-animal).

#### Bunnicorn

**Source**: Speak with Animals: Magical Beast Companions 1

This companion is available via the [Beast Speaker feat](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/beast-speaker/). The 11th-level mastery benefit is given if the character takes the [Beast Speaker Mastery feat](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/beast-speaker-mastery/).

**Prerequisite(s)**: [Good](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Good)-aligned, [Heal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/heal) 3 ranks

Starting Statistics

**Size** Tiny; **Speed** 60 ft.; **AC** +1 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** gore (1d3); **Ability Scores** **Str** 3, **Dex** 20, **Con** 9, **Int** 5, **Wis** 12, **Cha** 14; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent), racial skill bonus: +8 [Acrobatics](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/acrobatics) when jumping; **Special Attacks** [healing](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic#TOC-Conjuration-Healing) horn

9th-Level Advancement

**Size** Small; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** gore (1d4); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** -2, **Cha** +2; [Spell-Like Abilities](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Spell-Like-Abilities-Sp-) [detect evil](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/d/detect-evil) (at will)

Mastery (11th-Level)

**Spell-Like Abilities** [magic circle against evil](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/m/magic-circle-against-evil) (constant), [neutralize poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/n/neutralize-poison) (constant)

#### Healing Horn (Sp)

A bunnicorn can heal a creature of their choosing as a [standard action](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Standard-Actions) by touching their horn to a target. They may use this ability a number of times equal to their [Charisma](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Charisma-Cha-) modifier. They [heal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/h/heal) 1d6 [hit points](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Hit-Points) of damage per 2 HD they possess. They may not [heal](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/h/heal) themself in this way.

#### Chikfari

**Source**: Speak with Animals: Magical Beast Companions 1

This companion is available via the [Beast Speaker feat](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/beast-speaker/). The 11th-level mastery benefit is given if the character takes the [Beast Speaker Mastery feat](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/beast-speaker-mastery/).

**Prerequisite(s)**: [Knowledge](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/knowledge) (dungeoneering) 3 ranks

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 50 ft. climb 30 ft.; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6) or kick (2d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** 11, **Dex** 18, **Con** 13, **Int** 6, **Wis** 14, **Cha** 11; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), racial skill bonus: +10 [Acrobatics](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/acrobatics) when jumping; **Special Attacks** chikfari [poison](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/afflictions/poison) devastating kick

9th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8) or kick (2d8); **Ability Scores** **Str** +8, **Dex** -2, **Con** +4

#### Chikfari Poison Bite

**Type**: injury; *effect* 1 [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-) damage; *save* fortitude [Con](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based DC; *frequency* 1/round (6 rounds); *cure* 1 save

#### Devastating Kick

A chikfari’s massive rear legs are incredibly powerful (dealing +1 1/2 its [Strength](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Strength-Str-) modifier in damage and having a critical multiplier of x3. Whenever a chikfari hits a target of its size or smaller, it may make a free [bull rush](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Bull-Rush) attempt to knock the target away, though the chikfari cannot move with the target if it does.

#### Chimera

**Source**: Speak with Animals: Magical Beast Companions 1

This companion is available via the [Beast Speaker feat](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/beast-speaker/). The 11th-level mastery benefit is given if the character takes the [Beast Speaker Mastery feat](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/beast-speaker-mastery/).

**Prerequisite(s)**: Speak Draconic

Starting Statistics

**Size** Small; **Speed** 30 ft., fly 50 ft. (poor); **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d6), bite (1d4), gore (1d4), 2 claws (1d2); **Ability Scores** **Str** 7, **Dex** 16, **Con** 11, **Int** 4, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 10; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent); **CMD** +4 vs. [trip](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip); **Special Attacks** [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) (2d6, 20/10 ft.)

9th-Level Advancement

**Size** Medium; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d8), bite (1d6), gore (1d6), 2 claws (1d4); **Ability Scores** **Str** +4, **Dex** -2, **Con** +2; **Special Attacks** [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) 4d6, 30/15 ft.

Mastery (11th-Level)

**Size** Large; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (2d6), bite (1d8), gore (1d8), 2 claws (1d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** +8, **Dex** -2, **Con** +4; **Special Attacks** [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) (6d6, 40/20 ft.)

#### Breath Weapon (Su)

A chimera’s [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) depends on the color of its [dragon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Dragon) head, as summarized on the table below. Regardless of its type, a chimera’s [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) is usable once every 1d4 rounds, deals the damage listed in its advancement above, and allows a [Reflex](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Reflex) save for half damage. The save DC is [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based.

The range of the [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) is listed in the advancements above. The first number is for lines, the second for cones. For example, the base [chimera](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/chimera) deals 2d6 with their [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-). If they are a black- or blue-[dragon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/creature-types#TOC-Dragon) [chimera](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/monster-listings/magical-beasts/chimera), their [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) is a 20-foot line. Otherwise it is a 10-foot cone.

To determine a chimera’s head color and [breath weapon](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Breath-Weapon-Su-) randomly, roll 1d10 and consult the table below:

| d20 | Head Color | Breath Weapon |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1-2 | Black | Line of acid |
| 3-4 | Blue | Line of lightning |
| 5-6 | Green | Cone of acid |
| 7-8 | Red | Cone of fire |
| 9-10 | White | [Cone of cold](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/c/cone-of-cold) |

#### Exuded Mist (Su)

A hollow hound is constantly exuding a mist from their paws, tail and eyes. The cumulative mist that forms around them grants a constant 10% [concealment](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Concealment). This [concealment](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Concealment) does not stack with the [concealment](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Concealment) granted by [obscuring mist](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/magic/all-spells/o/obscuring-mist) or similar spells or from [natural](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus) fog or smoke.

#### Remorhaz

**Source**: Speak with Animals: Magical Beast Companions 1

**Prerequisite(s)**: [Endurance](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/feats/general-feats/endurance)

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 30 ft., [burrow](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Burrow-Ex-) 20 ft.; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (2d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** 10, **Dex** 18, **Con** 13, **Int** 5, **Wis** 12, **Cha** 10; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft. [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [tremorsense](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Tremorsense-Ex-) 60 ft., Immunities fire cold; **CMD** +4 vs. [grapple](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Grapple); **Special Attacks** [heat](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Heat-Ex-)

9th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +3 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (2d8); **Ability Scores** **Str** +6, **Dex** -2, **Con** +4

#### Heat (Su)

An enraged remorhaz generates heat so intense that anything touching its body takes 4d6 points of fire damage. Creatures striking a remorhaz with [natural attacks](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Natural-Attacks) or unarmed strikes are subject to this damage, but not creatures striking with melee weapons. The heat can melt or burn weapons any weapon that strikes a remorhaz is allowed a DC 19 [Fortitude](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Fortitude) save to avoid taking damage. The save DC is [Constitution](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/ability-scores#TOC-Constitution-Con-)-based. When the remorhaz companion grows to large size, the fire damage increases to 6d6.

**Size** Large; **Speed** 40 ft.; **AC** +4 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** bite (1d4), 2 claws (1d3); **Ability Scores** **Str** 16, **Dex** 11, **Con** 17, **Int** 1, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 5; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent).

4th-Level Advancement

**Ability Scores** **Str** +2, **Con** +2; **Special Qualities** [combat trained](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/handle-animal).

#### Shade Ferret

**Source**: [JBE:SPPC](http://www.opengamingstore.com/collections/jon-brazer-enterprises/products/jbesfpc)

**Special** A Small cavalier can choose this as a mount.

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 40 ft.; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** 2 claws (1d3), bite (1d4); **Ability Scores** **Str** 13, **Dex** 13, **Con** 15, **Int** 2, **Wis** 13, **Cha** 8; **Special Qualities** [blindsight](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities) 60 ft., [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent), stand on hind legs

Stand on Hind Legs (Ex)

When making a full attack, a shade ferret must stand on its hind legs. This causes the shade ferret to take a –2 penalty on all Reflex saves for the round.

4th-Level Advancement

**Ability Scores** **Str** +2, **Con** +2; **Special Qualities** [combat trained](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/handle-animal), superior scent

Superior Scent (Ex)

This ability functions like the scent ability except that it can detect an opponent within 120 feet. This range is increased to 240 feet when upwind and decreases to 60 feet when downwind. Strong and overpowering scents can still be detected at twice or three times their normal range, respectively. Additionally, this ability provides a +12 racial bonus to all Survival checks when tracking by scent.

#### Tazelwurm

**Source**: Speak with Animals: Magical Beast Companions 1

Starting Statistics

**Size** Medium; **Speed** 40 ft.; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** 2 claws (1d4), bite (1d10); **Ability Scores** **Str** 11, **Dex** 16, **Con** 12, **Int** 2, **Wis** 15, **Cha** 15; **Special Qualities** [darkvision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Darkvision) 60 ft., [low-light vision](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Low-Light-Vision), [scent](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/special-abilities#TOC-Scent), [tremorsense](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/bestiary/rules-for-monsters/universal-monster-rules#TOC-Tremorsense-Ex-) 60 ft., racial skill bonus +4 [Stealth](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/skills/stealth); **CMD** can’t be [tripped](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Trip); **Special Attacks** ambush

9th-Level Advancement

**Size** Large; **AC** +2 [natural armor](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Natural-Armor-Bonus); **Attack** 2 claws (1d6), bite (2d6); **Ability Scores** **Str** +8, **Dex** -2, **Con** +4

#### Ambush (Ex)

If a tazelwurm catches an opponent [flat-footed](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/conditions#TOC-Flat-Footed) it gains a +4 [circumstance bonus](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/basics-ability-scores/glossary#TOC-Circumstance-Bonus) to its [attack roll](https://www.d20pfsrd.com/gamemastering/combat#TOC-Attack-Roll) for that round.
